   bhikṣuṇī vinaya	BikzuNI  vinaya
   STORY OF MAHĀPRAJĀPATĪ GAUTAMĪ	STORY Oc MAHĀPRAt ĀPATĪ GAUTAMĪ
   1. oṃ namo buddhāya | āryamahāsāṃghikānāṃ lokottaravādināṃ	1. om namaH budDAya | Arya mahA sAMGikAnAm loka uttara vAdinAm
   madhy' udeśikānāṃ pāṭhena bhikṣuṇīvinaya	maDy a u deSikAnAm pAWena BikzuNI vinaya
   syādiḥ |	sya AdiH |
   bhagavān samyaksambuddho yadarthaṃ samudāgato tadartham abhisambhāvayitvā	BagavAn samyaksambudDaH yad arTam samudAgataH tad arTam aBisamBAvayitvA
   śākyeṣu viharati śākyānāṃ kapilavastusmin nyagrodhārāme śāstā devānāñ ca	SAkyezu viharati SAkyAnAm kapilavastusmin nyagroDa ArAme SAstA devAnAn ca
   manuṣyānāñ ca buddho bhagavān satkṛtogurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito arcito	manuzyAnAn ca budDaH BagavAn satkRta uguru kRtaH mAnitaH pUjitaH arcitaH 
   apacāyito lābhāgrayaśo 'graprāpto lābhī	apacAyitaH lABa agra yaSo  agra prAptaH lABI
   cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārānān | tatra	cIvara piNxapAta Sayana Asana glAna pratyaya BEzajya parizkArAnAn | tatra
   cānupalipto padmam iva jalena puṇyabhāgīyān satvān puṇyehi niveśayamāno	ca anupaliptaH padmam iva jalena puNya BAgIyAn satvAn puNya ihi niveSayamAnaH 
   phalabhāgīyān satvān phalehi pratiṣṭhāpayamāno vāsanābhāgīyān satvān	Pala BAgIyAn satvAn Pala ihi pratizWApayamAnaH vAsanA BAgIyAn satvAn
   vāsanāyām avasthāpayamāno amṛtam analpakena devamanuṣyān samvibhajanto	vAsanAyAm avasTApayamAnaH amRtam analpakena deva manuzyAn samviBajantaH 
   prāṇikoṭiniyutaśatasahasrāṇy amṛtaṃ anuprāpayanto	prANi kowi niyuta Sata sahasrANi amRtam anuprApayantaH 
   anavarāgrajātijarāmaraṇasaṃsārakāntāranarakavidurgān mahāprapātād	anavara agra jAti jarA maraNa saMsAra kAntAra naraka vidurgAt mahA prapAtAt 
   abhyuddharitvā kṣeme śive same sthale abhaye nirvāṇe pratiṣṭhāpayamāno	aByudDaritvA kzeme Sive same sTale aBaye nirvANe pratizWApayamAnaH 
   āvarjayitvā	AvarjayitvA
   aṅgamagadhavṛjimallikāśikośalakurupañcālacedivatsamatsyaśūrasenaśividaśārṇa	aFga magaDa vRjima llikA aSi koSala kuru paQcAla cedi vatsa matsya SUrasena Sivi daSa arNa
   cāsvakiavanti |	ca asvakiavanti |
   jñāne dṛṣṭaparākramo svayāṃbhūḥ divyehi vihārehi viharanto brāhmehi	jQAne dRzwa parAkramaH svayA aMBUH divya ihi vihAra ihi viharantaH brAhma Ihi
   vihārehi āryehi vihārehi aniñjehi vihārehi viharanto brāhmehi vihārehi	vihAra ihi Aryehi vihAra ihi aniQjehi vihAra ihi viharantaH brAhma ihi vihAra Ihi
   āryehi vihārehi aniñjehi vihārehi sātatye hi vihārehi buddho	Aryehi vihAra ihi aniQjehi vihAra ihi sAtatye hi vihAra ihi budDaH 
   buddhavihārehi jino jinavihārehi jānako jānakavihārehi sarvajño	budDa vihAra ihi jinaH jina vihAra ihi jAnakaH jAnaka vihAra ihi sarvajQaH 
   sarvajñavihārehi cetovasiparamapāramipraptāś ca punar buddhā bhagavanto	sarvajQa vihAra ihi cetaH vasi parama pArami praptAH ca punar budDAH BagavantaH 
   yehi yehi vihārehi ākāṅkṣanti tehi tehi vihārehi viharanti vihārakuśalāś	yehi yehi vihAra Ihi AkAFkzanti tehi tehi vihAra ihi viharanti vihAra kuSalAS
   ca punar buddhā bhagavantaḥ |	ca punar budDAH BagavantaH |
   2. atha khalu mahāprajāpatī gautamī cchandāya cchandakapālāya	2. aTa Kalu mahA prajApatI gOtamI cCandAya cCanda kapAlAya
   dāsacchandāye cchandakamātare ca pañcahi ca śākiyānīśatehi sārdhaṃ yena	dAsa= CandAye cCandaka mAtare ca paQca hi ca SAki yAnI Satehi sArDam yena
   bhagavāṃs tenopasaṃkramitvā bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte	BagavAn tena upasaMkramitvA BagavataH pAdO SirasA vanditvA ekAnte
   asthāsi ekāntasthitā mahāprajāpatī gautamī bhagavantam etad avocat |	asTA asi ekAnta sTitA mahA prajApatI gOtamI Bagavantam etat avocat |
   durlabho bhagavan buddhotpādo durlabhā saddharmadeśanā | bhagavāṃs	durlaBaH Bagavan budDa utpAdaH durlaBA sadDarma deSanA | BagavAn= 
   caitarhi loke utpanno tathāgato 'rhan samyaksambuddho dharmo ca deśayati	ca etarhi loke utpannaH taTAgataH arhan samyaksambudDaH DarmaH ca deSayati
   aupasamiko pārinivāṇiko sugatapravedito amṛtasya prāptaye nirvāṇasya	OpasamikaH pArinivANikaH sugata praveditaH amRtasya prAptaye nirvANasya
   sākṣātkriyāya samvartati | sādhu bhagavan mātṛgrāmo pi labheya	sAkzAt kriyAya samvartati | sADu Bagavat mAtR grAmaH pi laBeya
   tathāgatapravedite dharmavinaye pravrajyām upasampadaṃ bhikṣuṇibhāvaṃ |	taTAgata pravedite Darma vinaye pravrajyAm upasampadam BikzuNi BAvam |
   bhagavān āha | mā te gautami rocatu tathāgatapravedite dharmavinaye	BagavAn Aha | mA te gOtami rocatu taTAgata pravedite Darma vinaye
   pravrajyāmupasaṃpadā bhikṣuṇībhāvo |	pravrajyAm upasaMpadA BikzuNIBAvaH |
   atha khalu mahāprajāpatī gautamī | na khalu bhagavān mātṛgrāmasya avakāśaṃ	aTa Kalu mahA prajApatI gOtamI | na Kalu BagavAn mAtR grAmasya avakASam
   karoti tathāgata pravedite dharmavinaye pravrajyāmupasampadāya	karoti taTAgata pravedite Darma vinaye pravrajyAm upasampadAya
   bhikṣuṇībhāvāyeti | sā bhagavato pādau śirasā vanditvā sārdhaṃ cchandāya	BikzuNI BAvAya iti | sA BagavataH pAdO SirasA vanditvA sArDam cCandAya
   cchandakapālāye dāsacchandāye cchandakamātare ca yena tāni pañca	cCandakapAlAye dAsa= CandAye cCandaka mAtare ca yena tAni paQca
   śākiyānīśatāni tenopasaṃkramitvā śākiyānīyo etad avocat | na khalu	SAki yAnI SatAni tena upasaMkramitvA SAkiyAnIyaH etat avocat | na Kalu
   āryamiśrikāyo bhagavān avakāśaṃ karoti mātṛgrāmasya tathāgatapravedite	Arya miSrikAyaH BagavAn avakASam karoti mAtR grAmasya taTAgata pravedite
   dharmavinaye pravrajyāupasaṃpadāya bhikṣuṇībhāvāya | kim puna vayam	Darma vinaye pravrajyA aupasaMpadAya BikzuNI BAvAya | kim puna vayam
   āryamiśrikāyo sāmam eva keśān otārayitvā kāṣāyāni vastrāṇi ācchādayitvā	Arya miSrikAyaH sAmam eva keSAn otArayitvA kAzAyAni vastrANi AcCAdayitvA
   kośakābaddhehi yānehi bhagavantaṃ kośalehi janapadehi cārikāṃ caramāṇaṃ	koSaka AbadDA ihi yAn ehi Bagavantam koSala ihi janapadehi cArikAm caramANam
   pṛṣṭhimena pṛṣṭhim ābandhema | sace mo bhagavān anujāniṣyati pravrajiṣyāmo	pRzWimena pRzWim AbanDema | sace maH BagavAn anujAnizyati pravrajizyAmaH 
   no ca anujāniṣyati evam tu tāyi bhagavato santike brahmacaryañ cariṣyāmaḥ	no ca anujAnizyati evam tu tAyi BagavataH santike brahmacaryan carizyAmaH
   sādhu āryeti tāyo śākiyānīyo mahāprajāpatīye gautamīye pratyāśrauṣi |	sADu AryA iti tAyaH SAkiyAnIyaH mahA prajApatIye gOtamIye pratyASrOzi |
   3. atha khalu bhagavān kapilavastusmin nagare yathābhiramyaṃ viharitvā	3. aTa Kalu BagavAn kapilavastusmin nagare yaTA aBiramyam viharitvA
   kośaleṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ prakrāmi | atha khalu mahāprajāpatī gautamī	koSalezu janapadezu cArikAm prakrAmi | aTa Kalu mahA prajApatI gOtamI
   sārdhaṃ cchandāye cchandakapalāye dāsacchandāya cchandakamātare ca pañcahi	sArDam cCandAye cCandaka palAye dAsa= CandAya cCandaka mAtare ca paQca hi
   ca śākiyānīśatehi sātmaneva keśān otārayitvā kāṣāyāṇi vastrāṇi	ca SAki yAnI Satehi sA AtmanA iva keSAn otArayitvA kAzAyANi vastrANi
   ācchādayitvā kośakabaddhehi yānehi bhagavantaṃ kośaleṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ	AcCAdayitvA koSaka badDa ihi yAn ehi Bagavantam koSalezu janapadezu cArikAm
   caramāṇaṃ pṛṣṭhimena pṛṣṭham anubandheṃsuḥ |	caramANam pRzWimena pRzWam anubanDeMsuH |
   4. atha khalu bhagavān kośaleṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ caramāno mahatā	4. aTa Kalu BagavAn koSalezu janapadezu cArikAm caramAnaH mahatA
   bhikṣusaṃghena sārdhaṃ pañcahi bhikṣuśatehi yena kośalānāṃ śrāvastīnagaraṃ	Bikzu saMGena sArDam paQca hi Bikzu Sata ihi yena koSalAnAm SrAvastI nagaram
   tad avasāri | tad anuprāptas tatraiva viharati jetavane	tat avasAri | tat anuprAptaH tatra eva viharati jetavane
   anāthapiṇḍadasyārāme |	anATapiNxadasya ArAme |
   atha khalu mahāprajāpatī gautamī yena bhagavāṃs tenopasaṃkramitvā	aTa Kalu mahA prajApatI gOtamI yena BagavAn tena upasaMkramitvA
   bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte asthāsi | ekāntasthitā	BagavataH pAdO SirasA vanditvA ekAnte asTA asi | ekAnta sTitA
   mahāprajāpatī gautamī bhagavantam etad avocat | durlabho bhagavan	mahA prajApatI gOtamI Bagavantam etat avocat | durlaBaH Bagavan
   buddhotpādo durlabhā saddharmadeśanā | bhagavāṃś caitarhi loke utpanno	budDa utpAdaH durlaBA sadDarma deSanA | BagavAn ca etarhi loke utpannaH 
   tathāgato rhaṃ samyaksambuddho dharmo ca deśate aupasamiko ca	taTAgataH rham samyaksambudDaH DarmaH ca deSate OpasamikaH ca
   pārinirvāṇiko sugatapravedito amṛtasya prāptaye nirvāṇasya sākṣātkriyāya	pArinirvANikaH sugata praveditaH amRtasya prAptaye nirvANasya sAkzAtkriyAya
   samvartati | sādhu bhagavan mātṛgrāmo pi labheya tathāgatapravedite	samvartati | sADu Bagavat mAtR grAmaH pi laBeya taTAgata pravedite
   dharmavinaye pravrajyāmupasampadāṃ bhikṣuṇībhāvaṃ | evam ukte bhagavān	Darma vinaye pravrajyAm upasampadAm BikzuNI BAvam | evam ukte BagavAn
   mahāprajāpatīṃ gautamīm etad avocat | mā te gautamī rocatu mātṛgrāmasya	mahA prajApatIm gOtamIm etat avocat | mA te gOtamI rocatu mAtR grAmasya
   tathāgatapravedite dharmavinaye pravrajyāupasampadābhikṣuṇibhāvo |	taTAgata pravedite Darma vinaye pravrajyA upasampada aBikzuNi BAvaH |
   5. atha khalu mahāprajāpatī gautamī | na khalu bhagavān avakāśaṃ karoti	5. aTa Kalu mahA prajApatI gOtamI | na Kalu BagavAn avakASam karoti
   mātṛgrāmasya tathāgatapravedite dharmavinaye pravrajyāya upasampadāya	mAtR grAmasya taTAgata pravedite Darma vinaye pravrajyAya upasampadAya
   bhikṣuṇibhāvasyeti | sā bhagavato pādāṃ śirasā vanditvā jetavanasya	BikzuNiBAvasya iti | sA BagavataH pAdAm SirasA vanditvA jetavanasya
   ārāmadvārakoṣṭhakasamīpe rodamānī asthāsi pādāṇguṣṭhena bhūmiṃ vilikhantī	ArAma dvAra kozWaka samIpe rodamAnI asTA asi pAdANguzWena BUmim viliKantI
   | addaśāśi khu anyataro bhikṣur mahāprajāpatīṃ gautamīṃ jetavanasya	| addaSa ASi Ku anyataraH BikzuH mahA prajApatIm gOtamIm jetavanasya
   ārāmadvārakoṣṭhasamīpe rudamānīn tiṣṭhantīṃ pādāṅguṣṭhena bhūmiṃ	ArAma dvAra kozWa samIpe rudamAnIn tizWantIm pAdAFguzWena BUmim
   vilikhentīṃ dṛṣṭvā ca punar yenāyuṣmān ānando tenopasaṃkramitvā āyuṣmantam	viliKentIm dRzwvA ca punar yena AyuzmAn AnandaH tena upasaMkramitvA Ayuzmantam
   ānandam etad avocat | eṣā āyuṣman ānanda mahāprajāpatī gautamī jetavanasya	Anandam etat avocat | ezA Ayuzman Ananda mahA prajApatI gOtamI jetavanasya
   ārāmakoṣṭhakasamīpe rudamānī tiṣṭhati pādāṅguṣṭhena bhūmiṃ vilikhantī |	ArAma kozWaka samIpe rudamAnI tizWati pAdAFguzWena BUmim viliKantI |
   gacchāvusānanda jānehi kiṃ mahāprapatī gautamī rodīti |	gacCA= usAnanda jAna ihi kim mahA prapatI gOtamI rodI iti |
   6. atha khalu āyuṣmān ānando yena mahāprajāpatī gautamī tenopasaṃkramitvā	6. aTa Kalu AyuzmAn AnandaH yena mahA prajApatI gOtamI tena upasaMkramitvA
   mahāprajāpatīṃ gautamīm etad avocat | kiṃ gautami rudasi | evam ukte	mahA prajApatIm gOtamIm etat avocat | kim gOtami rudasi | evam ukte
   mahāprajāpatī gautamī āyuṣmantam ānandam etad avocat | alam me āryānanda	mahA prajApatI gOtamI Ayuzmantam Anandam etat avocat | alam me Arya Ananda
   ruṇṇena yatra hi nāma evaṃ durlabho buddhotpādo evaṃ durlabhā	ruNNena yatra hi nAma evam durlaBaH budDa utpAdaH evam durlaBA
   saddharmadeśanā | bhagavāṃś caitarhi loke utpanno tathāgato 'rhan	sadDarma deSanA | BagavAn ca etarhi loke utpannaH taTAgataH arhan
   samyaksambuddho dharmo deśīyati aupasamiko pārinirvāṇiko sugatapravedito	samyaksambudDaH DarmaH deSIyati OpasamikaH pArinirvANikaH sugata praveditaH 
   amṛtasya prāptaye nirvāṇasya sākṣātkriyāyai samvartati | na ca bhagavān	amRtasya prAptaye nirvANasya sAkzAt kriyAyE samvartati | na ca BagavAn
   avakāśaṃ karoti mātṛgrāmasya tathāgatapravedite dharmavinaye	avakASam karoti mAtR grAmasya taTAgata pravedite Darma vinaye
   pravrajyāyopasampadāya bhikṣuṇībhāvasya ścai sādhu tāvāryānanda	pravrajyAya upasampadAya BikzuNI BAvasya ScE sADu tO= Arya Ananda
   bhagavantaṃ yāca yathā labheya mātṛgrāmo pi tathāgatapravedite	Bagavantam yAca yaTA laBeya mAtR grAmaH pi taTAgata pravedite
   dharmavinaye pravrajyām upasampadāṃ bhikṣuṇībhāvaṃ |	Darma vinaye pravrajyAm upasampadAm BikzuNI BAvam |
   7. sādhu gautamīti āyuṣmān ānando mahāprajāpatīye gautamīye pratiśrutvā	7. sADu gOtamI iti AyuzmAn AnandaH mahA prajApatIye gOtamIye pratiSrutvA
   yena bhagavāṃs tenopasaṃkramitvā bhagavataḥ pādauśirasā vanditvā ekānte	yena BagavAn tena upasaMkramitvA BagavataH pAda OSirasA vanditvA ekAnte
   asthāsi | ekāntasthito āyuṣmān ānando bhagavantam etad avocat durlabho	asTA asi | ekAnta sTitaH AyuzmAn AnandaH Bagavantam etat avocat durlaBaH 
   bhagavan buddhotpādo durlabhā saddharmadeśanā bhagavān cetarhi loke	Bagavan budDa utpAdaH durlaBA sadDarma deSanA BagavAn cetarhi loke
   utpanno tathāgato 'rhan samyaksambuddho dharmo ca deśyate aupasamiko	utpannaH taTAgataH arhan samyaksambudDaH DarmaH ca deSyate OpasamikaH 
   pārinirvāṇiko sugatapravedito amṛtasya prāptaye nirvāṇasya sākṣātkriyāyai	pArinirvANikaH sugata praveditaH amRtasya prAptaye nirvANasya sAkzAtkriyAyE
   samvartati | sādhu bhagavan mātṛgrāmo pi labheya tathāgatapravedite	samvartati | sADu Bagavat mAtR grAmaH pi laBeya taTAgata pravedite
   dharmavinaye pravrajyām upadampadāṃ bhikṣuṇibhāvaṃ | evam ukte bhagavān	Darma vinaye pravrajyAm upadampadAm BikzuNi BAvam | evam ukte BagavAn
   āyuṣmantam ānandam etad avocat | mā te gautamīmātā rocatu mātṛgrāmasya	Ayuzmantam Anandam etat avocat | mA te gOtamImAtA rocatu mAtR grAmasya
   tathāgatapravedite dharmavinaye pravrajyāmupasampadā bhikṣuṇībhāvo |	taTAgata pravedite Darma vinaye pravrajyAm upasampadA BikzuNIBAvaH |
   8. atha khalv āyuṣmān ānando | bhagavān nāvakaśaṃ karoti mātṛgrāmasya	8. aTa Kalu AyuzmAn AnandaH | BagavAn na avakaSam karoti mAtR grAmasya
   tathāgata pravedite dharmavinaye pravrajyāupasaṃpadāye bhikṣuṇībhāvasyeti	taTAgata pravedite Darma vinaye pravrajyA aupasaMpadAye BikzuNI BAvasya iti
   | bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā yena mahāprajāpati gautamī	| BagavataH pAdO SirasA vanditvA yena mahA prajApati gOtamI
   tenopasaṃkramitvā mahāprajāpatīṃ gautamīm etad avocat | na khalu gautamī	tena upasaMkramitvA mahA prajApatIm gOtamIm etat avocat | na Kalu gOtamI
   bhagavān avakāśaṃ karoti mātṛgrāmasya tathāgatapravedite dharmavinaye	BagavAn avakASam karoti mAtR grAmasya taTAgata pravedite Darma vinaye
   pravrajyāyopasaṃpadāya bhikṣuṇībhāvāya | evam ukte mahāprajāpatī gautamī	pravrajyAya upasaMpadAya BikzuNI BAvAya | evam ukte mahA prajApatI gOtamI
   āyuṣmantam ānandam etad avocat | sādhu tāvāryānanda dvitīyaṃ pi	Ayuzmantam Anandam etat avocat | sADu tO= Arya Ananda dvitIyam pi
   bhagavantaṃ yāca yathā mātṛgrāmo pi labheya tathāgatapravedite	Bagavantam yAca yaTA mAtR grAmaH pi laBeya taTAgata pravedite
   dharmavinaye pravrajyāṃ upasaṃpadāṃ bhikṣuṇībhāvaṃ | sādhu gautamīti	Darma vinaye pravrajyAm upasaMpadAm BikzuNI BAvam | sADu gOtami iti
   āyuṣmān ānando dvitīyaṃ pi mahāprajāpatīye gautamīye pratiśrutvā yena	AyuzmAn AnandaH dvitIyam pi mahA prajApatIye gOtamIye pratiSrutvA yena
   bhagavān tenopasaṃkramitvā bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte asthāsi	BagavAn tena upasaMkramitvA BagavataH pAdO SirasA vanditvA ekAnte asTA asi
   | ekānte sthito āyuṣmān ānando bhagavantam etad avocat | durlabho bhagavan	| ekAnte sTitaH AyuzmAn AnandaH Bagavantam etat avocat | durlaBaH Bagavan
   buddhotpādo ti tad evaṃ sarvaṃ yāva bhikṣuṇībhāvo ti evam ukte bhagavān	budDa utpAdaH ti tat evam sarvam yAva BikzuNI BAvaH ti evam ukte BagavAn
   āyuṣmantam ānandam etad avocat | māte gautamī mātā rocatu mātṛgrāmasya	Ayuzmantam Anandam etat avocat | mAte gOtamI mAtA rocatu mAtR grAmasya
   tathāgatapravedite dharmavinaye pravrajyā upasaṃpadā bhikṣuṇībhāvo |	taTAgata pravedite Darma vinaye pravrajyA upasaMpadA BikzuNIBAvaH |
   saṃyathāpi nāmānanda sampanne yavakaraṇe ca kāraṇḍavaṃ nāma rogarājā ti	saMyaTA api nAma Ananda sampanne yava karaNe ca kAraNxavam nAma rogarAjA ti

   pratikramati | etaṃ prakaraṇaṃ bhikṣuṇīyo mahāprajāpatīye gautamīye	pratikramati | etam prakaraNam BikzuNIyaH mahA prajApatIye gOtamIye

   | tatra brahmacaryaṃ cariṣyaṃ | sā bhikṣuṇī bhikṣuṇīhi evam asya vacanīyā	| tatra brahmacaryam carizyam | sA BikzuNI BikzuNIhi evam asya vacanIyA

   dharmaṃ saṃghaṃ śikṣām uddeśaṃ samvāsaṃ saṃbhogaṃ śāstṛpadaṃ	Darmam saMGam SikzAm uddeSam samvAsam saMBogam SAstR padam

   bhikṣuṇīhi vucyamānā tam eva vastuṃ samādāya pratigṛhya tiṣṭheya na	BikzuNIhi vucyamAnA tam eva vastum samAdAya pratigRhya tizWeya na
   pratiniḥsareya | sā bhikṣuṇī bhikṣuṇīhi yāvat tṛtīyakaṃ samanugrāhitavyā	pratiniHsareya | sA BikzuNI BikzuNIhi yAvat tRtIyakam samanugrAhitavyA

   samanugrāhiyamāṇā vā samanubhāṣiyamāṇā vā taṃ vastuṃ pratiniḥsareya ity	samanugrAhiyamANA vA samanuBAziyamANAH vA tam vastum pratiniHsareya iti
